***шевелиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́ться</a> (2852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ševelítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошевелиться.html>пошевели́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевельнуться.html>шевельну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to stir, to budge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевеля́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sidétʹ ne <b>ševeljásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit without stirring</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́сь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ševelísʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look lively/slippy!; get a move on!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to awaken, to show signs of life</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">thoughts, feelings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to appear</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ševelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stir, move</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигаться.html>дви́гаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dvígatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевеля́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ševeljáščij</span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шезлонг.html>шезло́нг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šezlóng</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шезлонг.html>шезло́нга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шезлонг.html>шезло́нги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шезлонг.html>шезло́нгов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chaise longue</li>
<li>deck chair, beach chair (a folding chair with a wooden frame)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***шейный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шейный.html>ше́йный</a> (16086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шея.html>ше́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šéja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шейный.html>ше́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šéjnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> neck; cervical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шейный.html>ше́йный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:позвонок.html>позвоно́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéjnyj</b> pozvonók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cervical vertebra</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шейный.html>ше́йный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корсет.html>корсе́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šéjnyj</b> korsét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neck brace, cervical collar</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a> (8382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шьлкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šĭlkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">silki</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šolk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шелка́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шелко́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шёлковый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silk (fiber and fabric)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clothes made of silk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шелка́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кичиться.html>кичи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná vsegdá xodíla v <b>šelkáx</b> i kičílasʹ étim</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She always showed off wearing silk (clothes).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>something soft and pleasant for touching
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>Шёлк</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>воло́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лёг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>пле́чи</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Šólk</b> jejó volós néžno ljóg mne na pléči.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The silk of her hair gently lay down on my shoulders.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковистый.html>шелкови́стый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šelkovístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шелковица.html>шелкови́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šelkovíca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелковый.html>шёлковый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Velíkij šólkovyj putʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюхо.html>брю́хе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюхо.html>брю́хе</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:щелк.html>щёлк</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na brjúxe šólk, a v brjúxe - ščólk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>phrase: all hat and no cattle, lit.: belly (wrapped) in silk, and in the belly - just a click</i>)</li></ul>

***шельма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льма</a> (22909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schelme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szelma</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šélʹma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льмы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шельма.html>ше́льм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rascal, rogue, scoundrel</li></ol>

***шептать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепта́ть</a> (3503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šьpъtati</i>, of onomatopoeic origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šeptátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прошептать.html>прошепта́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шепнуть.html>шепну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whisper (to talk in a quiet voice)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>ше́пчущий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šépčuščij</span>)
